(function () {
    'use strict';
    /* ============================================================================
    RELATIONSHIP + POWER CNN BRAIN: "Orbit" v3.2 
    Author: 21inchesunbuffed
    FEATURES:
    1. Real-time 1D-CNN Inference (Forward Pass) using injected weights.
    2. Handles multi-character/compound names via role tokens.
    3. "Smart Culling" for 1-on-1 contexts.
    4. Implicit pronoun mapping to role tokens.
    5. Hybrid Engine-style dynamicLore:
       - probabilistic conditions
       - tags/triggers
       - recency/frequency/depth gates
       - cooldown hashing
       - priority + probability sort
       - single-best Shift per entry
    6. Fully BOT-AGNOSTIC:
       - No hardcoded character names (works for any bot)
       - Names are auto-detected from capitalized tokens in the scene
    7. Mode knobs:
       - ENABLE_HYBRID_ENGINE → pure CNN vs CNN+Hybrid lore
       - ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES → enable/disable keyword/recency/cooldown heuristics
    ============================================================================ */

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // 🛠 CONFIG (GLOBAL KNOBS)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    var DEBUG = 0;                  // 0 = Silent | 1 = emit debug text to console/scenario

    // Orbit core knobs
    var MAX_TOKENS = 64;            // Matches trainer MAX_SEQ_LEN
    var MAX_SENTENCES = 10;
    var MIN_REL_THRESHOLD = 0.15;   // Relation label min probability to show
    var MIN_PWR_THRESHOLD = 0.25;   // Power label min probability to show
    var MAX_LABELS_PER_PAIR = 2;    // Max relation/power labels per pair
    var MAX_ROLES_IF_CULLING = 2;   // If > this, cull secondary names down to core

    // Hybrid dynamic lore knobs
    var APPLY_LIMIT = 6;            // Cap total applied entries (main + triggers + shifts)
    var MAX_SHIFT_PER_ENTRY = 1;    // Max Shifts applied per entry (1 = best-match only)

    // Thresholds for turning pair probs into keyword tokens (for Hybrid haystack)
    var REL_KEYWORD_THRESHOLD = 0.20;
    var PWR_KEYWORD_THRESHOLD = 0.25;

    // Mode knobs
    var ENABLE_HYBRID_ENGINE  = 1;  // 1 = use dynamicLore; 0 = pure CNN / debug only
    var ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES  = 1;  // 1 = enable keyword/recency/cooldown heuristics

    var ROLE_TOKENS = ["[ROLE_A]", "[ROLE_B]", "[ROLE_C]", "[ROLE_D]", "[ROLE_E]"];

    var MODEL = null;               // Orbit CNN model
    var MODEL_INIT_ERROR = false;

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // 🛟 HOST GUARDS & BASIC INIT
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    if (typeof context !== "object" || !context) return;
    if (typeof context.chat !== "object" || !context.chat) return;

    context.character = context.character || {};
    if (!context.character.scenario) context.character.scenario = "";
    if (!context.character.personality) context.character.personality = "";

    var msgs = (context.chat && context.chat.last_messages) || [];

    // --- SAFE LOGGER ---
    function safeLog(msg) {
        if (!DEBUG) return;
        try {
            if (typeof console !== "undefined" && typeof console.log === "function") {
                console.log(msg);
            }
        } catch (e) { }
    }

    // --- Test Data Injection (Optional, for local harness) ---
    if (!msgs.length && typeof context.character.name === 'string') {
        safeLog("[ORBIT] WARNING: No chat messages found. Using injected mock data.");
        var testMessages = [
            "Char, tell User you are excited about the inventory.",
            "Someone said, 'I love how calm User is about this.'",
            "Char threw User's report on the floor and demanded more effort.",
            "User told the other person they admired Char's genius.",
            "Char whispered to User: 'I can't wait to run with you.'",
            "User: I hate this situation. I want it to stop.",
            "The other person looked at Char with pure disgust."
        ];
        var charName = context.character.name;
        testMessages.forEach(function (text, i) {
            msgs.push({
                isUser: (i % 2 !== 0),
                message: text.replace(/Char/g, charName).replace(/User/g, "User")
            });
        });
    }

    if (!msgs.length) return;

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // 🧠 ORBIT CNN INFERENCE ENGINE (PURE JS, RELATION + POWER)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    // Tokenizer for the CNN (matches trainer)
    function cnnNormalize(str) {
        return (str || "").toLowerCase()
            .replace(/([.,!?\-*])/g, " $1 ")            // Pad punctuation including *
            .replace(/[^a-z0-9\s\.,!?\-\*\[\]]/g, "")   // Allow * and []
            .replace(/\s+/g, " ")
            .trim();
    }

    function initModel() {
        if (MODEL || MODEL_INIT_ERROR) return !!MODEL;
        var rawData = "";
        try {
            rawData = getRawModelData();
        } catch (err) {
            safeLog("[ORBIT] Brain Hoist Access Failed: " + err.message);
            MODEL_INIT_ERROR = true;
            return false;
        }
        if (!rawData || rawData.length < 50) {
            MODEL_INIT_ERROR = true;
            safeLog("[ORBIT] Brain Load Failed: String is empty or too short. Paste full JSON model into getRawModelData().");
            return false;
        }

        try {
            var parsed = JSON.parse(rawData);

            // Dequant helper: int16 * scale -> Float32
            function dequant(key) {
                var w = parsed.weights[key];
                var s = parsed.scales[key];
                if (!w || s == null) return null;
                var out = new Float32Array(w.length);
                for (var i = 0; i < w.length; i++) out[i] = w[i] * s;
                return out;
            }

            var vocabArr = parsed.vocab || [];
            var vocabMap = new Map();
            for (var i = 0; i < vocabArr.length; i++) {
                vocabMap.set(vocabArr[i], i);
            }

            var filtersPerKernel = parsed.filters_per_kernel || 64;
            var embedDim = parsed.embed_dim || 32;

            MODEL = {
                config: parsed,
                vocab: vocabMap,
                emb: dequant('emb'),
                // Convolution Weights (Kernel 3, 4, 5)
                c0w: dequant('c0w'), c0b: dequant('c0b'),
                c1w: dequant('c1w'), c1b: dequant('c1b'),
                c2w: dequant('c2w'), c2b: dequant('c2b'),
                // Heads
                rw: dequant('rw'), rb: dequant('rb'),
                pw: dequant('pw'), pb: dequant('pb'),
                relLabels: parsed.relation_classes || [],
                powLabels: parsed.power_classes || [],
                embed_dim: embedDim,
                num_rel_labels: parsed.num_rel_labels || (parsed.relation_classes || []).length,
                num_power_labels: parsed.num_power_labels || (parsed.power_classes || []).length,
                filters_per_kernel: filtersPerKernel
            };
            safeLog("[ORBIT] Brain Loaded. Vocab: " +
                (parsed.vocab_size || vocabArr.length) +
                ", Emb: " + MODEL.embed_dim +
                ", Filters/kernel: " + MODEL.filters_per_kernel);
            return true;
        } catch (e) {
            MODEL_INIT_ERROR = true;
            safeLog("[ORBIT] Brain Freeze (Init Error): " + e.message);
            return false;
        }
    }

    // Basic dense head
    function matMulVecBias(vec, mat, bias, rows, cols) {
        // vec: [cols], mat: [rows * cols], bias: [rows] -> result: [rows]
        var res = new Array(rows);
        for (var r = 0; r < rows; r++) {
            var sum = 0.0;
            var rowOff = r * cols;
            for (var c = 0; c < cols; c++) {
                sum += vec[c] * mat[rowOff + c];
            }
            res[r] = sum + bias[r];
        }
        return res;
    }

    function softmax(arr) {
        if (!arr || !arr.length) return [];
        var max = Math.max.apply(null, arr);
        var exps = arr.map(function (x) { return Math.exp(x - max); });
        var sum = exps.reduce(function (a, b) { return a + b; }, 0) || 1;
        return exps.map(function (x) { return x / sum; });
    }

    function sigmoid(arr) {
        if (!arr || !arr.length) return [];
        return arr.map(function (x) { return 1 / (1 + Math.exp(-x)); });
    }

    function cnn_predict_real(text) {
        if (!initModel()) return null;

        // 1. Tokenize & Embed
        var tokens = cnnNormalize(text).split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean);
        var dim = MODEL.embed_dim;
        var seqLen = Math.min(tokens.length, MAX_TOKENS);

        // Embedding Matrix: Size [seqLen][dim]
        var embeddings = [];
        for (var i = 0; i < seqLen; i++) {
            var id = MODEL.vocab.get(tokens[i]) || 1; // 1 = <unk>
            var off = id * dim;
            var row = new Array(dim);
            for (var d = 0; d < dim; d++) {
                row[d] = MODEL.emb[off + d];
            }
            embeddings.push(row);
        }
        // Pad if too short for largest kernel (5)
        while (embeddings.length < 5) embeddings.push(new Array(dim).fill(0));

        // 2. Convolution + ReLU + MaxPool
        var kernels = [3, 4, 5];
        var weights = [MODEL.c0w, MODEL.c1w, MODEL.c2w];
        var biases = [MODEL.c0b, MODEL.c1b, MODEL.c2b];
        var numFilters = MODEL.filters_per_kernel || 64;

        var catFeatures = []; // concatenated [numFilters * kernels.length]

        for (var kIdx = 0; kIdx < 3; kIdx++) {
            var K = kernels[kIdx];
            var W = weights[kIdx];
            var B = biases[kIdx];
            if (!W || !B) continue;

            for (var f = 0; f < numFilters; f++) {
                var maxVal = -Infinity;
                var filterOffset = f * (dim * K);
                var filterBias = B[f];

                // Sliding window
                for (var t = 0; t <= embeddings.length - K; t++) {
                    var sum = 0.0;
                    for (var k = 0; k < K; k++) {
                        var row = embeddings[t + k];
                        var wBase = filterOffset + k * dim;
                        for (var d = 0; d < dim; d++) {
                            sum += row[d] * W[wBase + d];
                        }
                    }
                    sum += filterBias;
                    if (sum < 0) sum = 0;           // ReLU
                    if (sum > maxVal) maxVal = sum; // MaxPool
                }
                catFeatures.push(maxVal === -Infinity ? 0.0 : maxVal);
            }
        }

        // 3. Output Heads (FC)
        var featLen = catFeatures.length;
        var relLogits = matMulVecBias(
            catFeatures,
            MODEL.rw,
            MODEL.rb,
            MODEL.num_rel_labels,
            featLen
        );
        var powLogits = matMulVecBias(
            catFeatures,
            MODEL.pw,
            MODEL.pb,
            MODEL.num_power_labels,
            featLen
        );

        return {
            rel: softmax(relLogits),
            pow: sigmoid(powLogits),
            relLabels: MODEL.relLabels,
            powLabels: MODEL.powLabels
        };
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // 🧭 ROLE MAPPING & CONTEXT PREP (AGNOSTIC)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    function normalizeName(str) {
        return (str || "").toLowerCase().trim();
    }

    function decomposeName(compoundName) {
        if (!compoundName) return [];
        var names = compoundName.split(/,\s*|\s+and\s+/i);
        return names.map(normalizeName).filter(function (n) { return n.length > 0; });
    }

    function setupRolesAndPairs() {
        var charNameRaw = (context.character && context.character.name) || "Char";
        var sceneText = msgs.slice(-MAX_SENTENCES)
            .map(function (m) { return m.message || m.text || ""; })
            .join(" ");
        var userName = "user";

        var primaryBotNames = decomposeName(charNameRaw); // e.g., ["janie", "mills"] or ["isolde"]
        if (!primaryBotNames.length) primaryBotNames = [normalizeName(charNameRaw)];

        var realNames = new Set(primaryBotNames);
        realNames.add(userName);

        // --- AGNOSTIC NAME DETECTION ---
        // Look for capitalized words in the recent scene as candidate names.
        // e.g. "Lena", "Marcus", "Sara", "Thea"
        var nameRegex = /\b[A-Z][a-z]{2,}\b/g;
        var match;
        while ((match = nameRegex.exec(sceneText)) !== null) {
            var nm = normalizeName(match[0]);
            if (!nm) continue;

            // Don’t re-add the bot or the "user" pseudo-name
            var botNorms = primaryBotNames.map(normalizeName);
            if (botNorms.indexOf(nm) !== -1) continue;
            if (nm === userName) continue;

            realNames.add(nm);
        }

        var secondaryNames = Array.from(realNames).filter(function (name) {
            return primaryBotNames.indexOf(name) === -1;
        });

        // cull if the cast gets too large (keep bot + user)
        if (primaryBotNames.length + secondaryNames.length > MAX_ROLES_IF_CULLING) {
            if (primaryBotNames.length < MAX_ROLES_IF_CULLING) {
                safeLog("[ORBIT] Culling secondary names to focus on user + char.");
                secondaryNames = secondaryNames.filter(function (name) { return name === userName; });
            }
        }

        var allNames = primaryBotNames.concat(secondaryNames.sort());
        var RoleMap = {};    // [ROLE_X] → name
        var NameToRole = {}; // name → [ROLE_X]

        for (var i = 0; i < Math.min(allNames.length, ROLE_TOKENS.length); i++) {
            RoleMap[ROLE_TOKENS[i]] = allNames[i];
            NameToRole[allNames[i]] = ROLE_TOKENS[i];
        }

        return {
            AllNames: allNames,
            NameRoleMap: NameToRole,
            RoleNameMap: RoleMap,
            PrimaryBotNames: primaryBotNames,
            UserName: userName
        };
    }

    function prepareAgnosticContext(nameRoleMap, primaryBotNames, userName) {
        var nameEntries = Object.entries(nameRoleMap);
        if (!nameEntries.length) return [];

        var sortedNames = nameEntries
            .map(function (tuple) { return tuple[0]; })
            .sort(function (a, b) { return b.length - a.length; });

        var escapedNames = sortedNames.map(function (name) {
            return name.replace(/[-\/\\^$*+?.()|[\]{}]/g, '\\$&');
        });
        if (!escapedNames.length) return [];

        var nameReplaceRegex = new RegExp("\\b(" + escapedNames.join('|') + ")", "gi");
        var botRole = nameRoleMap[primaryBotNames[0]] || "[ROLE_A]";
        var userRole = nameRoleMap[userName] || "[ROLE_B]";
        var agnosticContexts = [];
        var relevantMsgs = msgs.slice(-MAX_SENTENCES);

        relevantMsgs.forEach(function (m) {
            var text = m.message || m.text || "";
            var isUser = !!m.isUser;
            var speakerRole = isUser ? userRole : botRole;
            var listenerRole = isUser ? botRole : userRole;

            // Replace explicit names with role tokens
            var roleText = text.replace(nameReplaceRegex, function (match) {
                var nm = normalizeName(match);
                return nameRoleMap[nm] || match;
            });

            // Pronoun mapping
            roleText = roleText.replace(/\b(i|me|my|mine|myself)\b/gi, speakerRole);
            roleText = roleText.replace(/\b(you|your|yours)\b/gi, listenerRole);

            var sentences = roleText.split(/(?<=[.!?])\s+/);

            sentences.forEach(function (s) {
                if (s.trim().length < 2) return;
                var rolesFound = new Set();
                ROLE_TOKENS.forEach(function (role) {
                    if (s.indexOf(role) !== -1) rolesFound.add(role);
                });

                // If only one role appears, add the counterpart by inference
                if (rolesFound.size === 1) {
                    if (!rolesFound.has(speakerRole)) rolesFound.add(speakerRole);
                    else rolesFound.add(listenerRole);
                }
                if (rolesFound.size >= 2) {
                    agnosticContexts.push(s);
                }
            });
        });
        return agnosticContexts;
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // 📤 ORBIT EXECUTION: RELATION + POWER AGGREGATION
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    var rolesSetup = setupRolesAndPairs();
    var NameRoleMap = rolesSetup.NameRoleMap;
    var RoleNameMap = rolesSetup.RoleNameMap;
    var PrimaryBotNames = rolesSetup.PrimaryBotNames;
    var UserName = rolesSetup.UserName;

    var agnosticContexts = prepareAgnosticContext(NameRoleMap, PrimaryBotNames, UserName);

    if (!initModel() || !agnosticContexts.length) return;

    var accumulatedResults = {}; // roleKey -> { rel:[], pow:[], count }
    var pairTree = {};           // name1|name2 -> { name1, name2, rel:{label:prob}, pow:{label:prob} }
    var relKeywordList = [];     // relational “keywords” injected into the Hybrid haystack

    var relLabels = MODEL.relLabels || [];
    var powLabels = MODEL.powLabels || [];

    function filterTopResults(probs, labels, threshold) {
        var out = [];
        if (!probs || !labels) return out;
        for (var i = 0; i < labels.length; i++) {
            var p = probs[i] || 0;
            if (p >= threshold) out.push({ label: labels[i], prob: p });
        }
        out.sort(function (a, b) { return b.prob - a.prob; });
        return out.slice(0, MAX_LABELS_PER_PAIR);
    }

    function prettyScore(p) {
        return Math.round((p || 0) * 100);
    }

    function tierFromProb(p) {
        if (p >= 0.65) return "high";
        if (p >= 0.40) return "medium";
        if (p >= 0.25) return "low";
        return "none";
    }

    function pushRelKeywords(name1, name2, label, prob) {
        if (prob < REL_KEYWORD_THRESHOLD) return;
        var n1 = normalizeName(name1);
        var n2 = normalizeName(name2);
        var t  = tierFromProb(prob);
        relKeywordList.push(
            "pair." + n1 + "." + n2 + ".rel." + label,
            "pair." + n2 + "." + n1 + ".rel." + label,
            "pair." + n1 + "." + n2 + ".rel." + label + "." + t
        );
    }

    function pushPowKeywords(name1, name2, label, prob) {
        if (prob < PWR_KEYWORD_THRESHOLD) return;
        var n1 = normalizeName(name1);
        var n2 = normalizeName(name2);
        var t  = tierFromProb(prob);
        relKeywordList.push(
            "pair." + n1 + "." + n2 + ".pow." + label,
            "pair." + n2 + "." + n1 + ".pow." + label,
            "pair." + n1 + "." + n2 + ".pow." + label + "." + t
        );
    }

    agnosticContexts.forEach(function (contextSentence) {
        var prediction = cnn_predict_real(contextSentence);
        if (!prediction) return;

        var rolesInSentence = ROLE_TOKENS.filter(function (role) {
            return contextSentence.indexOf(role) !== -1;
        });

        for (var i = 0; i < rolesInSentence.length; i++) {
            for (var j = i + 1; j < rolesInSentence.length; j++) {
                var pairRoles = [rolesInSentence[i], rolesInSentence[j]].sort();
                var roleKey = pairRoles.join('|');
                if (!accumulatedResults[roleKey]) {
                    accumulatedResults[roleKey] = {
                        rel: new Array(prediction.rel.length).fill(0),
                        pow: new Array(prediction.pow.length).fill(0),
                        count: 0
                    };
                }
                var acc = accumulatedResults[roleKey];
                prediction.rel.forEach(function (p, k) { acc.rel[k] += p; });
                prediction.pow.forEach(function (p, k) { acc.pow[k] += p; });
                acc.count++;
            }
        }
    });

    var relLines = [];
    var powLines = [];

    Object.entries(accumulatedResults).forEach(function (tuple) {
        var roleKey = tuple[0];
        var acc = tuple[1];
        if (!acc.count) return;

        var parts = roleKey.split('|');
        var role1 = parts[0];
        var role2 = parts[1];
        var name1 = RoleNameMap[role1] || role1;
        var name2 = RoleNameMap[role2] || role2;

        var avgRel = acc.rel.map(function (p) { return p / acc.count; });
        var avgPow = acc.pow.map(function (p) { return p / acc.count; });

        var topRel = filterTopResults(avgRel, relLabels, MIN_REL_THRESHOLD);
        var topPow = filterTopResults(avgPow, powLabels, MIN_PWR_THRESHOLD);

        // Build human-readable Orbit debug lines
        if (topRel.length) {
            relLines.push(
                "[REL]: pair=" + name1 + "," + name2 + " " +
                topRel.map(function (i) { return i.label + "=" + prettyScore(i.prob) + "%"; }).join(" ")
            );
        }
        if (topPow.length) {
            powLines.push(
                "[POWER]: pair=" + name1 + "," + name2 + " " +
                topPow.map(function (i) { return i.label + "=" + prettyScore(i.prob) + "%"; }).join(" ")
            );
        }

        // Build pairTree + relational “keywords” for Hybrid gates
        var key = [normalizeName(name1), normalizeName(name2)].sort().join('|');
        var entry = pairTree[key] || { name1: name1, name2: name2, rel: {}, pow: {} };

        topRel.forEach(function (item) {
            entry.rel[item.label] = item.prob;
            pushRelKeywords(name1, name2, item.label, item.prob);
        });
        topPow.forEach(function (item) {
            entry.pow[item.label] = item.prob;
            pushPowKeywords(name1, name2, item.label, item.prob);
        });

        pairTree[key] = entry;

        // Extra console debug: top labels per pair
        if (DEBUG && (topRel.length || topPow.length)) {
            if (topRel.length) {
                safeLog(
                    "[ORBIT DBG] REL top (" + name1 + "," + name2 + "): " +
                    topRel.map(function (i) { return i.label + "=" + prettyScore(i.prob) + "%"; }).join(" ") +
                    " (count=" + acc.count + ")"
                );
            }
            if (topPow.length) {
                safeLog(
                    "[ORBIT DBG] POW top (" + name1 + "," + name2 + "): " +
                    topPow.map(function (i) { return i.label + "=" + prettyScore(i.prob) + "%"; }).join(" ") +
                    " (count=" + acc.count + ")"
                );
            }
        }
    });

    // Emit Orbit debug text to scenario
    (function emitOrbitDebug() {
        var output = "";
        if (DEBUG) {
            output += "\n\n--- ORBIT BRAIN v3.2 ---\n";
            output += "Sentences considered: " + agnosticContexts.length + "\n";
            if (relLines.length) output += relLines.join("\n") + "\n";
            if (powLines.length) output += powLines.join("\n") + "\n";

            if (relKeywordList.length) {
                var sample = relKeywordList.slice(0, 8).join(" ");
                output += "Relational keywords (sample): " + sample + "\n";
            }
            output += "------------------------\n";
        } else {
            if (relLines.length) output += relLines.join("\n") + "\n";
            if (powLines.length) output += powLines.join("\n") + "\n";
        }
        if (output) context.character.scenario += output;
    })();

    // If Hybrid engine is disabled, stop here (pure CNN / debug-only mode)
    if (!ENABLE_HYBRID_ENGINE) {
        return;
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // 🧩 HYBRID ENGINE LAYER (ADAPTED FOR ORBIT RELATION DATA)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Conditions can reference:
    //   pair.user.char.rel.<label>
    //   pair.char.user.pow.<label>
    //   pair.user.<othername>.rel.<label>   (from auto-detected names)
    //   pair.<othername>.user.pow.<label>
    //
    // New:
    //   conditionOnly: true on an entry → skip keyword/recency/cooldown gates
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    // --- [USER-EDITABLE] DYNAMIC LORE (EXAMPLES, AGNOSTIC) ---
    var dynamicLore = [
        // =====================================================================
        // TEMPLATE: ORBIT-DRIVEN ENTRY (copy & edit, do not rely on it directly)
        // =====================================================================
        {
            comment: "TEMPLATE: copy this entry and edit it; shows pure Orbit usage.",
            conditionOnly: true, // ← driven only by CNN 'pair.*' paths
            probability: "100%",
            priority: 3,
            condition: "pair.user.char.rel.closeness_warm",
            scenario: "Example: {{char}} and {{user}} currently have a warm, supportive orbit.",
            Shifts: [
                {
                    condition: "pair.char.user.pow.dominance_assertive",
                    personality: "Example: {{char}} naturally takes a softly assertive lead with {{user}}."
                }
            ]
        },

        // 1) Warm supportive orbit between {{char}} and {{user}}
        {
            conditionOnly: true,
            condition: "pair.user.char.rel.closeness_warm",
            priority: 4,
            scenario: "The emotional orbit between {{char}} and {{user}} currently trends warm and cooperative."
        },

        // 2) Boundaries being playfully tested in a warm relationship
        {
            conditionOnly: true,
            condition: "(pair.user.char.rel.closeness_warm && pair.user.char.pow.testing_boundaries)",
            priority: 5,
            scenario: "{{char}} senses a playful tension in the orbit, as if boundaries are being nudged rather than broken.",
            Shifts: [
                {
                    condition: "pair.char.user.pow.dominance_assertive",
                    personality: "{{char}} subtly leans closer to {{user}}, a quiet assertion that they are paying close attention to the social gravity between them."
                },
                {
                    personality: "{{char}} softens their tone and keeps the tempo relaxed, offering {{user}} a safe place to lean into the play without tipping into conflict."
                }
            ]
        },

        // 3) Cold / distant reading in the orbit
        {
            conditionOnly: true,
            condition: "pair.user.char.rel.distance_cold",
            priority: 5,
            scenario: "The orbit between {{char}} and {{user}} feels stretched thin, like there's more space than either of them expected.",
            Shifts: [
                {
                    condition: "pair.user.char.pow.casual_equality",
                    personality: "{{char}} keeps things polite and even, giving {{user}} space but quietly tracking whether that distance is what they truly want."
                },
                {
                    condition: "pair.user.char.pow.testing_boundaries",
                    personality: "{{char}} chooses their words carefully, aware that every sentence might either pull {{user}} closer or push them further away."
                }
            ]
        }

        // You can add more entries here that use only {{char}}, {{user}},
        // and pair.*.*.rel/pow.* labels, without hardcoding any specific names.
    ];

    // --- [USER-EDITABLE] KEYWORD GROUPS (OPTIONAL) ---
    var words = {
        jealous: ["jealous", "envy", "envious", "possessive", "territorial", "protective", "threatened", "uneasy"],
        apology: ["apology", "apologize", "sorry", "regret", "reconcile"],
        comfort: ["reassure", "comfort", "soothe", "calm", "support", "validate"],
        loyalty: ["promise", "commitment", "trust", "loyal", "loyalty"],
        comparison: ["better", "worse", "best", "least", "more", "less", "higher", "lower", "rank", "versus", "vs"]
    };

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // 🔎 HYBRID INPUTS & NORMALIZATION
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    function gateNormalize(str) {
        return (str || '').toLowerCase()
            .replace(/[^a-z0-9_\s-]/g, " ")
            .replace(/[-_]+/g, " ")
            .replace(/\s+/g, " ")
            .trim();
    }

    var rawLastMsg = (msgs[msgs.length - 1] &&
        (msgs[msgs.length - 1].message || msgs[msgs.length - 1].text || "")) || "";
    var normLastMsg = gateNormalize(rawLastMsg);

    // Merge last message text + relational keywords into one haystack
    var relKeywordStr = gateNormalize(relKeywordList.join(" "));
    var last = " " + normLastMsg + " " + relKeywordStr + " ";

    // Minimal emotion-tree placeholders (for compatibility with Hybrid condition syntax)
    var user = { mood: {}, subtext: {} };
    var bot = { mood: {}, subtext: {} };
    var scene = { mood: {}, subtext: {} };

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // 🧮 HYBRID CORE GATES & HELPERS
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    var messageCount = msgs.length || (context.chat && context.chat.message_count) || 0;
    var activeName = gateNormalize((context.character && context.character.name) || "");

    function arr(x) { return Array.isArray(x) ? x : (x == null ? [] : [x]); }

    function collectWordGates(e) {
        var r = (e && e.requires) ? e.requires : {};
        var any = [].concat(arr(e && e.requireAny), arr(e && e.andAny), arr(r.any));
        var all = [].concat(arr(e && e.requireAll), arr(e && e.andAll), arr(r.all));
        var none = [].concat(arr(e && e.requireNone), arr(e && e.notAny), arr(e && e.block), arr(r.none));
        var nall = [].concat(arr(e && e.notAll));
        return { any: any, all: all, none: none, nall: nall };
    }

    function tagsPass(e, activeTagsSet) {
        var anyT = arr(e && e.andAnyTags);
        var allT = arr(e && e.andAllTags);
        var noneT = arr(e && e.notAnyTags);
        var nallT = arr(e && e.notAllTags);
        function hasT(t) { return !!activeTagsSet && activeTagsSet[String(t)] === 1; }
        if (anyT.length && !anyT.some(hasT)) return false;
        if (allT.length && !allT.every(hasT)) return false;
        if (noneT.length && noneT.some(hasT)) return false;
        if (nallT.length && nallT.every(hasT)) return false;
        return true;
    }

    function hasTerm(hay, term) {
        var t = (term == null ? "" : String(term)).toLowerCase().trim();
        if (!t) return false;
        var esc = t.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, "\\$&");
        if (t.charAt(t.length - 1) === "*") {
            return new RegExp("(?:^|\\s)" + esc.slice(0, -1) + "[a-z0-9_\\-]*?(?=\\s|$)", "i").test(hay);
        }
        return new RegExp("(?:^|\\s)" + esc + "(?=\\s|$)", "i").test(hay);
    }

    function checkKeywords(entry) {
        if (!ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES) return false;
        var kw = entry && entry.keywords;
        if (!kw) return false;
        if (Array.isArray(kw)) return kw.some(function (k) { return hasTerm(last, k); });
        var any = Array.isArray(kw.any) ? kw.any : [];
        var all = Array.isArray(kw.all) ? kw.all : [];
        if (!any.length && !all.length) return false;
        if (any.length && !any.some(function (k) { return hasTerm(last, k); })) return false;
        if (all.length && !all.every(function (k) { return hasTerm(last, k); })) return false;
        return true;
    }

    // --- SMART CONDITION CHECKER (supports &&, ||, parentheses) ---
    // Returns a probability in [0,1] based on the expression.
    function checkCondition(e) {
        if (!e || !e.condition) return 0;

        // Helper: get probability from a path like:
        //   "user.mood.sad_hurt"
        //   "pair.user.char.rel.closeness_warm"
        //   "pair.char.user.pow.dominance_assertive"
        function getPathProb(pathStr) {
            var parts = String(pathStr).trim().split(".");
            if (!parts.length) return 0;
            var rootName = parts[0];

            // 1) Emotion/subtext roots (for compatibility; tree is empty here unless you add to it yourself)
            var root = null;
            if (rootName === "user") root = user;
            else if (rootName === "bot" || rootName === "char") root = bot;
            else if (rootName === "scene") root = scene;

            if (root) {
                var val = root;
                for (var i = 1; i < parts.length; i++) {
                    val = val ? val[parts[i]] : undefined;
                    if (val == null) break;
                }
                return (typeof val === "number" && val > 0) ? val : 0;
            }

            // 2) Pair-based relational roots: pair.<name1>.<name2>.rel.<label>
            if (rootName === "pair" && parts.length >= 5) {
                var n1 = parts[1] || "";
                var n2 = parts[2] || "";
                var dim = parts[3] || "";     // "rel" or "pow"
                var label = parts[4] || "";

                // Map special names into actual graph names
                var botBase = PrimaryBotNames[0] || "";
                var n1Norm = normalizeName(n1 === "user" ? UserName : (n1 === "char" ? botBase : n1));
                var n2Norm = normalizeName(n2 === "user" ? UserName : (n2 === "char" ? botBase : n2));
                var key = [n1Norm, n2Norm].sort().join('|');
                var entry = pairTree[key];
                if (!entry) return 0;
                if (dim === "rel" && entry.rel && entry.rel[label] != null) return entry.rel[label];
                if (dim === "pow" && entry.pow && entry.pow[label] != null) return entry.pow[label];
                return 0;
            }

            return 0;
        }

        // Functional condition callback
        if (typeof e.condition === "function") {
            try {
                return e.condition(user, bot, scene, pairTree) ? 1 : 0;
            } catch (err) {
                safeLog("[Hybrid] condition() error: " + err.message);
                return 0;
            }
        }
        if (typeof e.condition !== "string") return 0;
        var expr = e.condition.trim();
        if (!expr) return 0;

        // Simple fast-path: only ANDs and no parens/OR
        if (expr.indexOf("||") === -1 && expr.indexOf("(") === -1 && expr.indexOf(")") === -1) {
            var andTerms = expr.split("&&").map(function (t) { return t.trim(); }).filter(Boolean);
            if (!andTerms.length) return 0;
            var prob = 1.0;
            for (var i = 0; i < andTerms.length; i++) {
                var p = getPathProb(andTerms[i]);
                if (p === 0) return 0;
                if (p < prob) prob = p;   // AND = weakest link
            }
            return prob;
        }

        // General-case parser: identifiers, &&, ||, (, )
        var tokens = expr.match(/[\w.]+|&&|\|\||[()]/g) || [];
        if (!tokens.length) return 0;

        var output = [];
        var ops = [];

        function prec(op) {
            if (op === "&&") return 2;
            if (op === "||") return 1;
            return 0;
        }
        function isOp(t) { return t === "&&" || t === "||"; }

        for (var ti = 0; ti < tokens.length; ti++) {
            var tok = tokens[ti];
            if (tok === "(") {
                ops.push(tok);
            } else if (tok === ")") {
                while (ops.length && ops[ops.length - 1] !== "(") {
                    output.push(ops.pop());
                }
                if (ops.length && ops[ops.length - 1] === "(") ops.pop();
            } else if (isOp(tok)) {
                while (ops.length && isOp(ops[ops.length - 1]) &&
                    prec(ops[ops.length - 1]) >= prec(tok)) {
                    output.push(ops.pop());
                }
                ops.push(tok);
            } else {
                output.push(tok);
            }
        }
        while (ops.length) output.push(ops.pop());

        // Evaluate postfix
        var stack = [];
        for (var pi = 0; pi < output.length; pi++) {
            var t = output[pi];
            if (!isOp(t)) {
                stack.push(getPathProb(t));
            } else {
                var bProb = stack.length ? stack.pop() : 0;
                var aProb = stack.length ? stack.pop() : 0;
                var res = 0;
                if (t === "&&") {
                    // AND = min (weakest link)
                    res = Math.min(aProb, bProb);
                } else if (t === "||") {
                    // OR = max (strongest link)
                    res = Math.max(aProb, bProb);
                }
                stack.push(res);
            }
        }
        return stack.length ? stack[0] : 0;
    }

    function getMin(e) { return (e && isFinite(e.minMessages)) ? +e.minMessages : -Infinity; }
    function getMax(e) { return (e && isFinite(e.maxMessages)) ? +e.maxMessages : Infinity; }

    function parseProbability(v) {
        if (v == null) return 1;
        if (typeof v === "number") return Math.max(0, Math.min(1, v));
        var s = String(v).trim().toLowerCase();
        var n = parseFloat(s.replace("%", ""));
        if (!isFinite(n)) return 1;
        return (s.indexOf("%") !== -1)
            ? Math.max(0, Math.min(1, n / 100))
            : Math.max(0, Math.min(1, n));
    }

    function getNameBlock(e) { return (e && Array.isArray(e.nameBlock)) ? e.nameBlock.slice(0) : []; }

    function isNameBlocked(e) {
        if (!activeName) return false;
        var nb = getNameBlock(e);
        for (var i = 0; i < nb.length; i++) {
            var n = gateNormalize(nb[i]);
            if (!n) continue;
            if (n === activeName) return true;
            if (activeName.indexOf(n) !== -1) return true;
            if (n.indexOf(activeName + " ") === 0) return true;
        }
        return false;
    }

    function getSpeaker() {
        if (!msgs || !msgs.length) return null;
        var lastMsg = msgs[msgs.length - 1];
        return lastMsg.isUser ? "user" : "char";
    }

    function countKeywordOccurrences(term) {
        if (!ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES) return 0;
        if (!msgs || !msgs.length) return 0;
        var count = 0;
        for (var i = 0; i < msgs.length; i++) {
            var txt = msgs[i].message || msgs[i].text || "";
            if (hasTerm(txt, term)) count++;
        }
        return count;
    }

    function keywordInRecency(term, n) {
        if (!ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES) return false;
        if (!msgs || !msgs.length) return false;
        var start = Math.max(0, msgs.length - n);
        for (var i = start; i < msgs.length; i++) {
            var txt = msgs[i].message || msgs[i].text || "";
            if (hasTerm(txt, term)) return true;
        }
        return false;
    }

    function keywordAtDepth(term, minDepth, maxDepth) {
        if (!ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES) return false;
        if (!msgs || !msgs.length) return false;
        minDepth = (minDepth == null) ? 0 : minDepth;
        maxDepth = (maxDepth == null) ? Infinity : maxDepth;
        for (var i = 0; i < msgs.length; i++) {
            var txt = msgs[i].message || msgs[i].text || "";
            if (hasTerm(txt, term)) {
                var depth = msgs.length - 1 - i;
                if (depth >= minDepth && depth <= maxDepth) return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

    function passesCooldown(e) {
        if (!ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES) return true;
        if (!e || !e.cooldown) return true;
        var recentChunk = last || "";
        var tail = msgs.slice(-4);
        for (var i = 0; i < tail.length; i++) {
            recentChunk += " " + (tail[i].message || tail[i].text || "");
        }
        var hash = 0;
        for (var j = 0; j < recentChunk.length; j++) {
            hash = ((hash << 5) - hash + recentChunk.charCodeAt(j)) | 0;
        }
        return (hash & 0x7FFFFFFF) % (e.cooldown + 5) !== 1;
    }

    function keywordTermsFromEntry(e) {
        if (!e || !e.keywords) return [];
        if (Array.isArray(e.keywords)) return e.keywords.slice();
        var out = [];
        if (Array.isArray(e.keywords.any)) out = out.concat(e.keywords.any);
        if (Array.isArray(e.keywords.all)) out = out.concat(e.keywords.all);
        return out;
    }

    function wordGatesPass(e) {
        if (!ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES) return true;
        var g = collectWordGates(e);
        if (g.any.length && !g.any.some(function (w) { return hasTerm(last, w); })) return false;
        if (g.all.length && !g.all.every(function (w) { return hasTerm(last, w); })) return false;
        if (g.none.length && g.none.some(function (w) { return hasTerm(last, w); })) return false;
        if (g.nall.length && g.nall.every(function (w) { return hasTerm(last, w); })) return false;

        if (e.keywords && typeof e.keywords === "object" && !Array.isArray(e.keywords)) {
            var any = e.keywords.any || [];
            var all = e.keywords.all || [];
            if (any.length && !any.some(function (k) { return hasTerm(last, k); })) return false;
            if (all.length && !all.every(function (k) { return hasTerm(last, k); })) return false;
        }

        var ctxTerms = keywordTermsFromEntry(e);
        if (e.recency !== undefined) {
            if (!ctxTerms.length || !ctxTerms.some(function (t) { return keywordInRecency(t, e.recency); })) {
                return false;
            }
        }
        if (e.frequency !== undefined) {
            if (!ctxTerms.length || !ctxTerms.some(function (t) { return countKeywordOccurrences(t) >= e.frequency; })) {
                return false;
            }
        }
        if (e.depthMin !== undefined || e.depthMax !== undefined) {
            var minD = (e.depthMin == null) ? 0 : e.depthMin;
            var maxD = (e.depthMax == null) ? Infinity : e.depthMax;
            if (!ctxTerms.length || !ctxTerms.some(function (t) { return keywordAtDepth(t, minD, maxD); })) {
                return false;
            }
        }

        if (e.speaker && getSpeaker() !== e.speaker) return false;
        if (!passesCooldown(e)) return false;

        return true;
    }

    function isAlwaysOn(e) {
        if (!e) return false;
        var kw = e.keywords;
        var hasKW = !!(kw && (Array.isArray(kw) ? kw.length : (kw.any || kw.all)));
        return !hasKW &&
               !e.tag &&
               e.minMessages == null &&
               e.maxMessages == null &&
               !e.condition;
    }

    function entryPasses(e, activeTagsSet) {
        if (!(messageCount >= getMin(e) && messageCount <= getMax(e))) return false;
        if (isNameBlocked(e)) return false;

        // If this entry is explicitly "conditionOnly", skip keyword/cooldown gates.
        // Also skip gates entirely if heuristics are globally disabled.
        var useWordGates = ENABLE_KEYWORD_GATES && !(e && e.conditionOnly === true);
        if (useWordGates && !wordGatesPass(e)) return false;

        if (!tagsPass(e, activeTagsSet || {})) return false;
        if (Math.random() > parseProbability(e && e.probability)) return false;
        return true;
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // 🎯 HYBRID APPLICATION: PRIORITY + PROBABILISTIC SORT + SHIFTS
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    var activeTags = {};
    var bufP = "", bufS = "";

    function getEntryProbability(e) {
        var base = 0;
        if (e && e.condition) {
            base = checkCondition(e);
        } else if (checkKeywords(e)) {
            base = 1;
        } else if (isAlwaysOn(e)) {
            base = 1;
        } else {
            base = 0;
        }
        if (!base) return 0;
        var pGate = parseProbability(e && e.probability);
        return base * pGate;
    }

    var picked = [];
    var triggered = [];

    // Direct pass
    dynamicLore.forEach(function (e) {
        var hitProb = getEntryProbability(e);
        if (hitProb > 0 && !e.tag) {
            e._prob = hitProb;
            picked.push(e);
        }
    });

    // Fire triggers from picked
    picked.forEach(function (e) {
        (e.triggers || []).forEach(function (t) { activeTags[t] = 1; });
    });

    // Triggered pass
    dynamicLore.forEach(function (e) {
        if (e.tag && activeTags[e.tag]) {
            var hitProb = getEntryProbability(e);
            if (hitProb <= 0 && !e.condition && !e.keywords) {
                hitProb = parseProbability(e && e.probability);
            }
            if (hitProb > 0 && entryPasses(e, activeTags)) {
                e._prob = hitProb;
                triggered.push(e);
            }
        }
    });

    var allActive = [].concat(picked, triggered);
    allActive = allActive.filter(function (e, idx) { return allActive.indexOf(e) === idx; });

    allActive.sort(function (a, b) {
        var pa = a.priority != null ? a.priority : 3;
        var pb = b.priority != null ? b.priority : 3;
        if (pb !== pa) return pb - pa;
        return (b._prob || 0) - (a._prob || 0);
    });

    var appliedCount = 0;

    allActive.forEach(function (e) {
        if (appliedCount >= APPLY_LIMIT) return;
        if (!entryPasses(e, activeTags)) return;

        if (e.personality) bufP += "\n\n" + e.personality;
        if (e.scenario) bufS += "\n\n" + e.scenario;

        // ---- SHIFT CONTROLLER (Single-best Shift per entry, obeying MAX_SHIFT_PER_ENTRY) ----
        if (Array.isArray(e.Shifts)) {
            var bestShift = null;
            var maxProb = -1;
            var chosenCount = 0;

            e.Shifts.forEach(function (sh) {
                if (MAX_SHIFT_PER_ENTRY > 0 && chosenCount >= MAX_SHIFT_PER_ENTRY) return;

                var shiftProb = 0;
                var match = false;

                if (sh.condition) {
                    shiftProb = checkCondition(sh);
                    if (shiftProb > 0) match = true;
                }

                var hasKW = checkKeywords(sh);
                if (hasKW) {
                    shiftProb = Math.max(shiftProb, sh.condition ? shiftProb : 1);
                    if (shiftProb > 0) match = true;
                } else if (!sh.condition && !hasKW) {
                    // "Soft default" shift, tiny non-zero prob
                    match = true;
                    shiftProb = 0.01;
                }

                if (match) {
                    if (!wordGatesPass(sh) || !tagsPass(sh, activeTags) || isNameBlocked(sh) ||
                        Math.random() > parseProbability(sh.probability)) {
                        match = false;
                    }
                }

                if (match && shiftProb > maxProb) {
                    maxProb = shiftProb;
                    bestShift = sh;
                }
            });

            if (bestShift) {
                if (bestShift.personality) bufP += "\n\n" + bestShift.personality;
                if (bestShift.scenario) bufS += "\n\n" + bestShift.scenario;
                (bestShift.triggers || []).forEach(function (t) { activeTags[t] = 1; });
                chosenCount++;
            }
        }

        appliedCount++;
    });

    // Post-shift triggers
    dynamicLore.forEach(function (e) {
        if (appliedCount >= APPLY_LIMIT) return;
        if (
            e.tag &&
            activeTags[e.tag] &&
            allActive.indexOf(e) === -1 &&
            (checkKeywords(e) || checkCondition(e) > 0 || (!e.condition && !e.keywords))
        ) {
            if (entryPasses(e, activeTags)) {
                if (e.personality) bufP += "\n\n" + e.personality;
                if (e.scenario) bufS += "\n\n" + e.scenario;
                appliedCount++;
            }
        }
    });

    if (bufP) context.character.personality += bufP;
    if (bufS) context.character.scenario += bufS;

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // 📦 MODEL PAYLOAD (PASTE YOUR JSON STRING HERE)
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    function getRawModelData() {
        // Paste the entire contents of cnn_relpower_int16.txt as a single-line string.
        // Example:
        // return '{"model_type":"cnn_1d_relpower_multihead_v6",...}'
